Source Code

These source-code files were obtained by digitally photographing an Artemis 72 program listing from a private collection and then modifying pre-existing Comanche 55 (Apollo 11) source files to incorporate changes. Photography was by Ron Burkey, and transcription was performed by a team of volunteers. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that additional images may be available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP: ASSEMBLE REVISION 072 OF AGC PROGRAM ARTEMIS 
	BY NASA 2021114-011 11:40 FEB. 26, 1971
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

001541,000002:                                                                                                  #  Copyright:    Public domain.
001542,000003:                                                                                                  #  Filename:     ERASABLE_ASSIGNMENTS.agc
001543,000004:                                                                                                  #  Purpose:      Part of the source code for Artemis (i.e., Colossus 3),
001544,000005:                                                                                                  #                build 072.  This is for the Command Module's (CM) 
001545,000006:                                                                                                  #                Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC), we believe for 
001546,000007:                                                                                                  #                Apollo 15-17.
001547,000008:                                                                                                  #  Assembler:    yaYUL

Page 38 

001565,000026:                                                                                                  #  CONVENTIONS AND NOTATIONS UTILIZED FOR ERASABLE ASSIGNMENTS.
001566,000027: 
001567,000028:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  IS USED IN TWO WAYS.  IT IS OFTEN USED TO CHAIN A GROUP
001568,000029:                                                                                                  #                OF ASSIGNMENTS SO THAT THE GROUP MAY BE MOVED WITH THE
001569,000030:                                                                                                  #                CHANGING OF ONLY ONE CARD.  EXAMPLE:
001570,000031: 
001571,000032:                                                                                                  #                                        X       EQUALS  START
001572,000033:                                                                                                  #                                        Y       EQUALS  X       +SIZE.X
001573,000034:                                                                                                  #                                        Z       EQUALS  Y       +SIZE.Y
001574,000035: 
001575,000036:                                                                                                  #                (X, Y, AND Z ARE CONSECUTIVE AND BEGIN AT START.       )
001576,000037:                                                                                                  #                (SIZE.X AND SIZE.Y ARE THE RESPECTIVE SIZES OF X AND Y,
001577,000038:                                                                                                  #                 USUALLY NUMERIC,  IE. 1, 2, 6, 18D, ETC.              )
001578,000039: 
001579,000040: 
001580,000041:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  OFTEN IMPLIES THE SHARING OF REGISTERS (DIFFERENT NAMES
001581,000042:                                                                                                  #                AND DIFFERENT DATA).  EXAMPLE:
001582,000043: 
001583,000044:                                                                                                  #                                        X       EQUALS  Y
001584,000045: 
001585,000046: 
001586,000047:                                                                                                  #        = MEANS THAT MULTIPLE NAMES HAVE BEEN GIVEN TO THE SAME DATA.
001587,000048:                                                                                                  #                (THIS IS LOGICAL EQUIVALENCE, NOT SHARING)  EXAMPLE.
001588,000049: 
001589,000050:                                                                                                  #                                        X       =       Y
001590,000051: 
001591,000052: 
001592,000053:                                                                                                  #        THE SIZE AND UTILIZATION OF AN ERASABLE ARE OFTEN INCLUDED IN
001593,000054:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMENTS IN THE FOLLOWING FORM.  M(SIZE)N.
001594,000055: 
001595,000056:                                                                                                  #                M REFERS TO THE MOBILITY OF THE ASSIGNMENT.
001596,000057:                                                                                                  #                     B   MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED BY BASIC
001597,000058:                                                                                                  #                         INSTRUCTIONS AND THUS IS E-BANK SENSITIVE.
001598,000059:                                                                                                  #                     I   MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED ONLY BY
001599,000060:                                                                                                  #                         INTERPRETIVE INSTRUCTIONS, AND IS THUS E-BANK
001600,000061:                                                                                                  #                         INSENSITIVE AND MAY APPEAR IN ANY E-BANK.
001601,000062: 
001602,000063:                                                                                                  #                SIZE IS THE NUMBER OF REGISTERS INCLUDED BY THE SYMBOL.
001603,000064: 
001604,000065:                                                                                                  #                N INDICATES THE NATURE OF PERMANENCE OF THE CONTENTS.
001605,000066:                                                                                                  #                     PL MEANS THAT THE CONTENTS ARE PAD LOADED.
001606,000067:                                                                                                  #                     DSP MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED FOR A DISPLAY.
001607,000068:                                                                                                  #                     PRM MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS PERMANENT, IE. IT
001608,000069:                                                                                                  #                         IS USED DURING THE ENTIRE MISSION FOR ONE
001609,000070:                                                                                                  #                         PURPOSE AND CANNOT BE SHARED.
001610,000071:                                                                                                  #                     TMP MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED TEMPORARILY OR
001611,000072:                                                                                                  #                         IS A SCRATCH REGISTER FOR THE ROUTINE TO WHICH
001612,000073:                                                                                                  #                         IT IS ASSIGNED.  THAT IS, IT NEED NOT BE SET
001613,000074:                                                                                                  #                         PRIOR TO INVOCATION OF THE ROUTINE NOR DOES IT
001614,000075:                                                                                                  #                         CONTAIN USEFUL OUTPUT TO ANOTHER ROUTINE.  THUS

Page 39 

001616,000077:                                                                                                  #                         IT MAY BE SHARED WITH ANY OTHER ROUTINE WHICH
001617,000078:                                                                                                  #                         IS NOT ACTIVE IN PARALLEL.
001618,000079:                                                                                                  #                     IN  MEANS INPUT TO THE ROUTINE AND IT IS PROBABLY
001619,000080:                                                                                                  #                         TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001620,000081:                                                                                                  #                     OUT MEANS OUTPUT FROM THE ROUTINE, PROBABLY
001621,000082:                                                                                                  #                         TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001622,000083:

Page 40

001625,000086:                                                                                                  #        SPECIAL REGISTERS.
001626,000087: 
001627,000088: ???????                        A                  EQUALS   0                                     
001628,000089: ???????                        L                  EQUALS   1                                     #  L AND Q ARE BOTH CHANNELS AND REGISTERS.
001629,000090: ???????                        Q                  EQUALS   2                                     
001630,000091: ???????                        EBANK              EQUALS   3                                     
001631,000092: ???????                        FBANK              EQUALS   4                                     
001632,000093: ???????                        Z                  EQUALS   5                                     #  ADJACENT TO FBANK AND BBANK FOR DXCH Z
001633,000094: ???????                        BBANK              EQUALS   6                                     #  (DTCB) AND DXCH FBANK (DTCF)
001634,000095:                                                                                                  #  REGISTER 7 IS A ZERO-SOURCE, USED BY ZL.
001635,000096:

001640,000101: ???????                        ZRUPT              EQUALS   15                                    #  (13 AND 14 ARE SPARES.)
001641,000102: ???????                        BANKRUPT           EQUALS   16                                    #  USUALLY HOLDS FBANK OR BBANK
001642,000103: ???????                        BRUPT              EQUALS   17                                    #  RESUME ADDRESS AS WELL.

003010,001471:                                                                                                  #  IS USED DURING CALLS TO THE EXECUTIVE AND WAITLIST - THE RUPTREGS ARE NOT.

003288,001749:                                                                                                  #  DESIRES TO BYPASS THE CHANNEL REPRESENTATION, HE SHOULD LOAD C31FLWRD   VIA V21 N01 TO THE VALUES SHOWN IN THE
003289,001750:                                                                                                  #  FOLLOWING TABLES:
003290,001751: 
003291,001752:                                                                                                  #     A VALUE      MEANING FOR CHANNEL 31                                     B VALUE      MEANING FOR CHANNEL 33
003292,001753: 
003293,001754:                                                                                                  #     0 OR 4       BITS 15,14, + 13 OF CHANNEL 31 ARE VALID                   0 OR 4       BITS 4 + 5 OF CHANNEL 33
003294,001755:                                                                                                  #     1            G&N CONTROL FREE                                           1 OR 5       OPTICS MODE CMC
003295,001756:                                                                                                  #     2            G&N CONTROL ATT. HOLD                                      2 OR 6       OPTICS MODE ZERO
003296,001757:                                                                                                  #     3            G&N CONTROL AUTO                                           3 OR 7       OPTICS MODE MANUAL
003297,001758:                                                                                                  #     5            SCS CONTROL FREE

003299,001760:                                                                                                  #     7            SCS CONTROL AUTO
